name:Sâ€uâ€mâ€mâ€eâ€râ€eâ€tâ€e
info:Superior Double Room
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:51 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 9, 2024
msg:I stayed in Luzhou for one night when I passed by. I didn't want to go into the city. I happened to see that there was a Holiday Inn, so I stayed there for one night. This time changed my impression of Holiday Inn. I often stayed in Holiday Inn from 2008 to 2014. Later, in 2021, I stayed in Holiday Inn in Chengde out of nostalgia. As a result, I was very disappointed. The room was old and the check-in was very slow... At that time, I thought, "Has the old hotel fallen into such a state?" This time I stayed in Holiday Inn in Luzhou. I felt that the quality of Holiday Inn was still online. The hotel was easy to find, there were plenty of parking spaces, and the underground parking lot was clean and bright. George at the front desk did his job on the day of check-in. The room equipment was relatively new, the breakfast was very good, and the Chinese and Western food were of high quality. I also ate Gulin handmade noodles that I didn't eat last time I came to Luzhou.
The only drawback is that it is a bit noisy, and the sound insulation effect of the glass curtain wall is a bit weak. After all, it is on the edge of the second ring road, and there are many cars. I sleep well, so it doesn't affect much. If you sleep lightly, you should have a room facing the community!
